TestPolicyQuotaController_CheckQuota\n**Purpose**: Verify the CheckQuota method works correctly\n\n**Test Cases**:\n- ✅ No quota exceeded when count is 0\n- ✅ No quota exceeded when count is below max (4 out of 5)\n- ✅ Quota exceeded when count equals max (5 out of 5)\n- ✅ Quota is tracked independently per namespace\n\n**Expected Behavior**:\n- Returns `nil` error when count < max\n- Returns error with message \"policy quota exceeded\" when count >= max\n- Different namespaces maintain independent counts\n\n### 2. TestPolicyQuotaController_Run\n**Purpose**: Verify the event processing loop\n\n**Test Cases**:\n- ✅ Sync events are processed without error\n- ✅ Upsert events increment the policy count\n- ✅ Delete events decrement the policy count\n- ✅ Quota is enforced correctly after events\n- ✅ Counts are accurate after multiple operations\n\n**Expected Behavior**:\n- Count starts at 0\n- Each Upsert increments count by 1\n- Each Delete decrements count by 1\n- Quota checking reflects the current count\n\n### 3. TestPolicyQuotaController_MultipleNamespaces\n**Purpose**: Verify isolation between namespaces\n\n**Test Cases**:\n- ✅ Two namespaces maintain independent counts\n- ✅ Adding a policy to one namespace doesn't affect another\n- ✅ Each namespace has its own quota limit\n\n**Expected Behavior**:\n- Namespaces are completely isolated\n- ns-1 and ns-2 can each have policies up to the limit\n- Exceeding quota in one namespace doesn't affect others\n\n### 4. TestPolicyQuotaController_MaxQuotaEdgeCases\n**Purpose**: Verify edge cases with extreme quota values\n\n**Test Cases**:\n- ✅ Max quota of 1 is enforced correctly\n- ✅ First policy is allowed\n- ✅ Second policy exceeds quota with max=1\n\n**Expected Behavior**:\n- CheckQuota() returns nil for empty namespace\n- After adding one policy, quota is exceeded\n- Error message correctly shows current count and max\n\n## Integration Testing\n\nTo test the controller within the Cilium daemon:\n\n1. **Enable the Cell**: Add the PolicyQuotaController cell to your hive configuration\n2. **Watch Events**: The controller will automatically watch for CiliumNetworkPolicy events\n3. **Monitor Logs**: Check logs for policy-quota subsystem messages\n\nExample log output:\n```\ntime=\"2025-03-02T10:00:00Z\" level=info msg=\"PolicyQuotaController started\" subsys=policy-quota\ntime=\"2025-03-02T10:00:01Z\" level=debug msg=\"CiliumNetworkPolicy resource synced\" subsys=policy-quota\ntime=\"2025-03-02T10:00:02Z\" level=debug msg=\"CiliumNetworkPolicy upserted\" subsys=policy-quota namespace=default policyName=test-policy-1 count=1 max=10\n```\n\n## Manual Testing\n\n### Using the Controller Directly\n\n```go\npackage main\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"log\"\n\n\tcilium_v2 \"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/policy/quota\"\n)\n\nfunc main() {\n\t// Create a controller with max 5 policies per namespace\n\tcontroller := quota.NewPolicyQuotaController(5, nil)\n\n\t// Manually set counts for testing\n\tcontroller.Mu.Lock()\n\tcontroller.NamespacePolicyCounts[\"test-ns\"] = 4\n\tcontroller.Mu.Unlock()\n\n\t// Check quota - should return nil\n\terr := controller.CheckQuota(\"test-ns\")\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tlog.Fatal(err)\n\t}\n\tlog.Println(\"✓ 4 policies out of 5 allowed\")\n\n\t// Now add one more policy\n\tcontroller.Mu.Lock()\n\tcontroller.NamespacePolicyCounts[\"test-ns\"] = 5\n\tcontroller.Mu.Unlock()\n\n\t// Check quota - should return error\n\terr = controller.CheckQuota(\"test-ns\")\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\tlog.Fatal(\"Expected error\")\n\t}\n\tlog.Printf(\"✓ Quota exceeded: %v\\n\", err)\n}\n```\n\n## Expected Error Messages\n\nWhen quota is exceeded, the controller returns:\n```\npolicy quota exceeded for namespace \"test-ns\": current count 5, maximum allowed 5\n```\n\n## Performance Considerations\n\n1. **Lock Contention**: The RWMutex protects the namespace counts map\n   - Read operations (CheckQuota) use RLock for parallel access\n   - Write operations (Upsert/Delete) use Lock for exclusive access\n\n2. **Memory Usage**:\n   - One entry per namespace with policies\n   - Entries are cleaned up when namespace policy count reaches zero\n\n3. **Event Processing**:\n   - Non-blocking event processing with concurrent goroutines\n   - Each event is independent and can be processed concurrently\n\n## Debugging Tips\n\n1. **Enable Debug Logging**: Set log level to DEBUG to see detailed events\n2. **Check Namespace Counts**: Use the RLock to safely inspect the map\n3. **Verify Events**: Use the fakeResource in tests to simulate events\n\n## Integration with Cilium\n\nThe PolicyQuotaController integrates with Cilium's resource watching framework:\n\n1. **Resource Events**: Watches `resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]`\n2. **Event Types**:\n   - `resource.Sync`: Initial sync of all policies\n   - `resource.Upsert`: Policy created or updated\n   - `resource.Delete`: Policy deleted\n\n3. **Thread Safety**: Uses proper locking for concurrent access\n\n## Future Enhancements\n\nPotential improvements for future versions:\n\n1. **Configurable Limits**: Allow per-namespace quotas via annotations\n2. **Quota Metrics**: Export Prometheus metrics for quota usage\n3. **Webhook Validation**: Reject policies before they're stored if quota exceeded\n4. **Event Notifications**: Send alerts when quota is near limit\n5. **Audit Logging**: Track quota violations for compliance\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Problem: Controller doesn't start\n- Check if Kubernetes API server is reachable\n- Verify resource.Resource[T] is properly initialized\n- Check logs for initialization errors\n\n### Problem: Quota not enforced\n- Verify controller is running (check logs)\n- Ensure resource events are being processed\n- Check namespace name matches exactly\n\n### Problem: Incorrect counts\n- Check for race conditions (ensure locks are held)\n- Verify Upsert/Delete events are being processed\n- Inspect the namespacePolicyCounts map directly\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":7,"cache_creation_input_tokens":785,"cache_read_input_tokens":89803,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":785},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"6ca055d5-2aee-479f-8bf0-1e6f0f61c52d","uuid":"2f13f4b9-e4b9-49b9-9bb9-5ef8d7c1e0a1"}

should return error\n\terr = controller.CheckQuota(\"test-ns\")\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\tlog.Fatal(\"Expected error\")\n\t}\n\tlog.Printf(\"✓ Quota exceeded: %v\\n\", err)\n}\n```\n\n## Expected Error Messages\n\nWhen quota is exceeded, the controller returns:\n```\npolicy quota exceeded for namespace \"test-ns\": current count 5, maximum allowed 5\n```\n\n## Performance Considerations\n\n1. **Lock Contention**: The RWMutex protects the namespace counts map\n   - Read operations (CheckQuota) use RLock for parallel access\n   - Write operations (Upsert/Delete) use Lock for exclusive access\n\n2. **Memory Usage**:\n   - One entry per namespace with policies\n   - Entries are cleaned up when namespace policy count reaches zero\n\n3. **Event Processing**:\n   - Non-blocking event processing with concurrent goroutines\n   - Each event is independent and can be processed concurrently\n\n## Debugging Tips\n\n1. **Enable Debug Logging**: Set log level to DEBUG to see detailed events\n2. **Check Namespace Counts**: Use the RLock to safely inspect the map\n3. **Verify Events**: Use the fakeResource in tests to simulate events\n\n## Integration with Cilium\n\nThe PolicyQuotaController integrates with Cilium's resource watching framework:\n\n1. **Resource Events**: Watches `resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]`\n2. **Event Types**:\n   - `resource.Sync`: Initial sync of all policies\n   - `resource.Upsert`: Policy created or updated\n   - `resource.Delete`: Policy deleted\n\n3. **Thread Safety**: Uses proper locking for concurrent access\n\n## Future Enhancements\n\nPotential improvements for future versions:\n\n1. **Configurable Limits**: Allow per-namespace quotas via annotations\n2. **Quota Metrics**: Export Prometheus metrics for quota usage\n3. **Webhook Validation**: Reject policies before they're stored if quota exceeded\n4. **Event Notifications**: Send alerts when quota is near limit\n5. **Audit Logging**: Track quota violations for compliance\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Problem: Controller doesn't start\n- Check if Kubernetes API server is reachable\n- Verify resource.Resource[T] is properly initialized\n- Check logs for initialization errors\n\n### Problem: Quota not enforced\n- Verify controller is running (check logs)\n- Ensure resource events are being processed\n- Check namespace name matches exactly\n\n### Problem: Incorrect counts\n- Check for race conditions (ensure locks are held)\n- Verify Upsert/Delete events are being processed\n- Inspect the namespacePolicyCounts map directly\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

Policy Deletion Flow\n\n```\nUser deletes CiliumNetworkPolicy\n        │\n        ▼\nKubernetes API Server removes policy\n        │\n        ▼\nresource.Resource detects event\n        │\n        ▼\nController receives Delete event\n        │\n        ▼\nhandleDelete decrements namespace count\n        │\n        ▼\nIf count reaches 0, remove namespace entry\n```\n\n## Thread Safety Model\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  PolicyQuotaController              │\n├─────────────────────────────────────┤\n│                                       │\n│ └─────────────────────────────────┘ │\n│                                       │\n└─────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## Event Processing
